<gmapID>0x80dbff95dcb58b03:0x3a4071a4be9adf3a< /gmapID>< Review>
We had a major pipe leak underneath our house earlier this year.  We actually had water come up through our floor heating vents...total disaster.

We had done two remodels in the house in the past ten years, done by two different contractors.  It didn't help that our house is 30 years old.  We have had three different "water events" in the past five years, and were on the verge of being cancelled by our insurance company.

One of the things I learned is that plumbers, like insurance companies use cute or funny ads on TV to gain market share, but the are all pretty much the same.  We had two different plumbing companies come in to fix the problem. The leaks continued.  We have pretty nice house, so the bids to fix the problem

were all over the map.  The 3rd plumber was from the remediation company, and in my view the only honest one, told us about epoxy coating.  He said it was a far better alternative than repiping our entire house.

Enter Bill Brink and Brinks services.

Bill Brinks came out personally to inspect our home.  His bid was prompt and a bit eye opening, but it was thorough and easy to understand, and definitely not scribbled on a pink form. I check a couple of references, and they were impeccable.  We had to leave our home for a week, as the amount of pipes and equipment and trucks was pretty overwhelming..  They did a through job of protecting our home, and in the end, we were very happy with the result.  His epoxy coating has a lifetime warranty,, and his fixtures have a ten year manufactures warranty.

Bill Brinks is a man of great integrity, with a great staff of plumbers, with really large trucks!

I highly reccomend his company.</Review>

< review>
About 3 years ago my dog, an 8 year old female chow, was diagnosed with hip dysplasia and severe arthritis in her elbows. Needless to say that she wasn’t able to walk much and regularly had limped after walking. At that time she was on all the joint supplements, pain killers and anti-inflammatories, and periodic shots of Adequan. About a year ago my Vetenarian had recommended that she undergo laser treatments for her hips and elbows. Since my Vet did not do this I searched around and found out that the Ambassador Vetenarian Hospital did perform laser treatments. My dog has been getting these laser treatments every week. For the past year she has been getting much better which I mostly attribute to these laser treatments. She’s more playful now, can stand on her feet longer, and has taken more and longer walks. She bugs me all the time to walk her which I do almost every day now. Just a few days ago while working her she actually started to run with me in tow holding her leash. Something she has not done in over 5 years. I stopped running her after 30 seconds for fear that she may start limping again. But to my astonishment the limping never happened. If your dog or cat is experiencing joint issues I highly recommend getting laser treatments at the Ambassador Vetenarian Hospital. My go to person there to administrate these treatments is Brien who has been giving my dog her treatments since day one. He is very knowledgeable of my dogs joint issues and has been doing an excellent and thorough job every time.</review>

The only reason for my two star review is for the service of the three vet techs that helped me which they deserve all 5 stars!!! Unfortunately I am rating the entire business. One senior receptionist is awfully rude, has no interest in your pets need. She would cut me off to ask for my contact info which is fair but to me, she was my messenger to the vet to get an understanding of the situation and showed no interest on what was going on.

I dropped off my two dogs for surgery which I had confirmed the previous day and per this receptionist, I didn't have an appointment. After standing there for about 20 min confused because I HAD confirmed my appointment she decides to say "Oh never mind, I see it". Many issues came along with this, one them losing my spay form that covered the entire expense and this is where one of the vet techs gets 5 stars, after arguing with the receptionist about my form being given to them and per her "IT WAS ON ME", vet tech stepped in and told me that she will hunt it down but either way to enjoy my day, I did not need to wait and if they don't find it they will help me with the cost. The receptionist did not look happy. Only one dog was spayed at the time and the other dog was pre-paid for. We continued to take our dogs for regular vaccines and flea treatment. For a few visits I did not have to communicate with the receptionist but when I did, she would always find something to try to start an issue.

I took our second dog to get her final vaccine and I was told by this receptionist I was over charged and had a balance in my account. I told her I was not over charged and I know I had a balance because I pre-paid for my dogs spay. She doesn't say anything. She then repeats no, its a separate overcharge for x amount. I tell her okay, include in today’s fees. She denied to include it and denied me a refund. I asked what will that overcharge be used for and tells me anything I pay for in the clinic, so once again I tell her to include it in the vaccines I was paying for my second dog. She gave me the finger signaling to wait and said she was trying to see where the overcharge was and who did it. I told her to that on her own time because unfortunately my second dog cannot see another dog and I would rather get out of there ASAP to avoid any issues. She refused to include it in the balance for the vaccines and had to investigate. I asked for a supervisor which was busy at the time so she said "It’s on you, you can wait but you're saying yourself you can’t stay so if you leave you leave" and as I was speaking she walked out the door and went to the main office.  I was frustrated, left to drop off the dog, came back to speak to a supervisor.

When I came back there was a supervisor waiting for me. She saw the overcharge and with no question or interest in who overcharged me, she gave me a refund. She definitely showed interest in the situation but her solution was to avoid the receptionist touching my file and that was the solution to it all. I told her the other techs and she were extremely helpful and caring but I was not going to return. I was going to get my dog spayed because I had paid but that was it. I took my dog the next morning to get spayed, they told me the latest to pick up was 7 but they will phone once she's ready. Never received a call. 630 I CALLED and my dog had been ready since 2PM. Why couldn't they call four hours ago?
That was it.

I did not like that I had to give my dog to them and wait in another room so they can give them vaccines and from observation anyone with a serious problem was not in the room while they examined their pets. My dog is my child and just like my human child I want to be there while they tell me the possibilities of what can be going on.

Once again, three girls were awesome!!!

I am now going to another vet and they are amazing! Communicate very well and all vet staff are awesome.< /text>

< Text>
My mother saw a dog in need of rescue at the Downey shelter and asked me to go get her. The problem was this particular dog was sick; sick dogs cannot fly so I needed a place that would board her. I called for hours trying to find any place that had isolated boarding for dogs with a fever and Ambassador Long Beach Vet Hospital was the only one in LA County that I found that would take her. The rescue dog had to stay for a week before she was healthy enough to fly to her new home. Had it not been for this vet hospital, she would have been put down. Not only did they make her healthy, they groomed her and she looked like a new dog. This story had a happy ending.< /Text>

< text>
I recently brought my dwarf bunny in for a very horrible eye infection.  The doctor was awesome, let me sit in for his shots, and most importantly, my bunny was better within a couple of days!  All of the workers are awesome, and they truly care about the health of the animals.  It was hard for me to find a vet who treated "exotic pets," so I was very lucky to stumble on this one!
Lastly, I suggested this vet to my mom because our cocker spaniel had been coughing and sneezing for years.  We took her to three different vets around the lakewood/long beach area, and every doctor assumed it was bronchitis or some sort of cold.  No treatments ever worked on her.  After my mom took her to this vet, we found out she has an enlarged heart and heart murmurs.  No vet had ever told us this before! She had been taking unnecessary medications for months!  I am so thankful we finally have a diagnosis!  Great vet, great prices.
P.S. I felt that I should mention that this vet did not try to give my pets any expensive unnecessary treatments.  He gave me exactly what my pet needed.  In other words, this vet isn't out to get your money, they are truly there to help your animals!< /text>

< user_name>
Andrea Dougherty< /user_name>
< Text>
They saved my disabled son's companion dog! Our 3 year old rescue dog needed life saving surgery and I was quoted over $2000 by VCA and would need to see a specialist. That is way out of our family budget. I decided to ask friends on Facebook about recommendations for other vets in our area and I chose to try Ambassador. I am so happy we did!!!! They literally saved our dog's life. The owner Dr. Sam performed the surgery for significantly less than what I was quoted and charges way less per visit on a regular basis than VCA. They are loving, kind and compassionate to both my dog and myself. When I sit in the waiting room I am not waiting more than 5 minutes for my dog to be seen. The other people in the waiting room all tell me they love the animal hospital. There are nothing but positive things to say about this place. Angelo is by far the best tech around! <Review>Pros: Friendly, attentive staff
Cons: Parking lot is small

I first came to Ambassador Long Beach Veterinary Hospital in the summer of 2006 to get my new puppy vaccinated. I found out about this place by looking online and comparing vaccination prices for all of the local vets. This place had the most affordable Puppy Wellness Plan that made getting all of the required vaccinations easy. I liked how helpful and friendly everyone was and how they really do treat your pet like it was their own. After I had my puppy vaccinated, they helped me with the next steps: spaying/neutering and licensing. After this positive experience, I said that I would take all of my future pets here.

<Date>1528585566052</Date><rate>5</rate><text>Great neighborhood brewery and homebrew shop. It is a friendly and casual atmosphere with a staff who knows the beer. A nice place to stop for a pint or a flight.

The beers were good all around. I especially liked the Cascadian IPA. The Bear Heart Scotch ale is a good example of a style that I wish we saw more of.  They have a diverse range of IPAs to go with the current trend, but enough other styles that there is something for all craft beer fans.

My only complaint is that they call their traditional English Pale Ale 'Edinburgh.' You either get that, or you don't.

< Text>
So I have been toying around with the idea of starting a home brew since all my friends and co workers have been doing it for awhile now and today I took the leap! I found Bear Roots Brewing was close to where I was at so I decided to give it shot. I walked in and was instantly welcomed by the staff, I was kind of over whelmed looking around at all the inventory they have and felt a little over my head at first because I had no idea what to get or how much or really anything at all that pertains to starting a home brew...That feeling didn't last long, as the staff helped me all the way through the whole process from start to finish. They hooked me up! I almost feel like I could give some one a lesson or two after everything I learned. I am so happy I found this place and will definitely be returning and bringing my friends so they can capitalize on this awesome hidden gem in Vista like I have. I also saw that they will not only be selling home brew supplies but will also be serving beer they them selves have brewed! I cant wait to come in a drink some beer and pick up some things for my next brew batch. One stop is all it took and im hooked! Check this place out for sure.< /Text>

[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPNWzZF9Su8jm3D-FAynOGmMAzcUOp_M7IwUqn6=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]<//Pics>

<user_id>105506874620980505888</user_id><user_name>Rebecca Hassinger<//user_name>< time>
1559122646856<//time>
< Rate>
4< /Rate>
<Review>I haven't been to many ball parks, but this place seems fine to me. It's shockingly clean for the number of people coming through and they serve a good variety of decent-quality food, including all of the classics - corn dogs, hot dogs, funnel cake, churros, nachos, BBQ... I will say that parking is very expensive - $15 at our last visit. We typically pick up free vouchers for seats at local businesses and then park a few blocks away to avoid paying. Exercise is good for you. The freebie seats are benches with backs, which isn't terrible. They are also located right behind home plate, which is rad. The staff are very attentive and helpful. They'll pick you out right quick if you're looking lost and can point you toward your seats. They maintain a good presence - not too invasive, but there to break up a fight, if one were to start up.
The minor league Giants seem like a good team and we always have fun watching them. The field has an LED playback board and a secondary electronic board showing number and speed of pitches. They have lots of little activities between the innings to include kids in the sport, which is cool. They do seem to have the same ones every time, but hey, it just builds traditions, right? All the staples are there - an announcer, musical cues, a clowning mascot (Gigante is awesome), and they always acknowledge holidays and bring some kid up to completely slaughter our national anthem (as it should be; you're not singing it right if you don't sing it wrong - loud and proud!).</Review>< pictures>
None<//pictures>

<review>Same park, just a new name. Evening and night games are wonderful. Close to the field and lots of activities between innings. Gigante is one of the best mascots around.

<name>Sandra Rosas Olden< /name><date>1532223152611</date>< rate>
3<//rate>
<review>I went for their Friday night fireworks. That was awesome.  The game was okay . It would be better if they used a different netting to protect the spectator's . The thick black one they have up makes it hard to see the game and forget about trying to keep your eye on the  ball because you can't see that either. The food was pricey and one beer cost what you would  pay for a 6 pack. The parking was $15 but if you go on a night with no fireworks it cost $10. The ticket prices start @ $12 for general admission, those are the bleacher seats and about $20 for assigned seating. I purchased the $20 assigned seats and regretted it about 20 minutes into the game. The seats were as uncomfortable as the bleachers and the sun was in my face for most of the game. My recommendation to you for a better experience than mine is; purchase bleacher seats and take a cushion for your booty, eat a big azz meal before going and if you have to enjoy the game with a buzz have a designated driver and drink before you go. One more thing, they have games you can participate and win prizes for. Make sure you play the tennis ball throw for big prizes like a trip to Hawaii. For the newbies, like I was, let me tell you how to play because they don't bother explaining. You purchase  a bag full of numbered tennis balls for $5 and at the end of the game you will be throwing your balls from the stands onto the field. The object of the game is to try and make your ball into the designated area to win the prize. And there you go my visit to the San Jose Giants game in a nut shell. :)</review><pics>None< /pics><Resp>None<//Resp>< gmap_id>
